Switzerland is famed for its breathtaking Alpine scenery, azure lakes, quaint medieval towns and thriving economy. Below are the top 4 destinations in Switzerland:\n\nThe city of Lucerne \nThe city of Lucerne is situated on the shores of the picturesque Lake Lucerne, home to the world-famous Chapel Bridge. The old town\u2019s architecture dating back to the 17th century, clock tower, lion statue, makes Lucerne an idyllic tourist city. Visitors can stroll along the lake, take in the magnificent mountain views or savor traditional Swiss cuisine.\n\nGeneva\nGeneva, the capital of the canton of Geneva, is the largest city in Switzerland. The city boasts unique Renaissance and Baroque architecture alongside countless upscale restaurants and hotels.\n\nThe charming village of Zermatt\nThe charming village of Zermatt lies at the foot of the iconic Matterhorn peak. It is a paradise for skiing and mountaineering. Visitors can admire Zermatt\u2019s breathtaking views from atop Gornergrat at 3,089m when taking the cable car ride. The traditional wood houses with red rooftops make a memorable impression.\n\nInterlaken\nInterlaken is a popular resort town nestled between two jewel-toned lakes, Thun and Brienz. V\u1eadn may c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 to ho\u1eb7c nh\u1ecf, c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 t\u1edbi nhanh ho\u1eb7c r\u1ea5t l\u00e2u m\u1edbi gh\u00e9 th\u0103m ta. \n\nCh\u01a1i game kh\u00f4ng ch\u1ec9 ch\u01a1i m\u00e0 c\u00f2n ph\u1ea3i ngh\u0129. Game \u0111\u1eddi l\u00e0 \u0111\u1ec9nh cao c\u1ee7a s\u1ef1 t\u01b0 duy. \nKhi b\u1ea1n n\u00e9m x\u00fac x\u1eafc t\u00ecm v\u1eadn may trong l\u01b0\u1ee3t ch\u01a1i, b\u1ea1n \u0111ang t\u01b0 duy nh\u01b0 con b\u1ea1c. \nKhi b\u1ea1n \u0111\u1ed5 x\u00fac x\u1eafc t\u00ecm c\u01a1 h\u1ed9i tr\u00ean b\u00e0n c\u1edd, b\u1ea1n \u0111ang t\u01b0 duy nh\u01b0 m\u1ed9t ng\u01b0\u1eddi ch\u01a1i. \nKhi t\u01b0 duy \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c m\u1ed9t l\u00e0 ki\u1ec3u n\u00e0o, s\u1ebd ch\u01a1i tr\u00ean b\u00e0n c\u1edd n\u00e0o th\u00ec vi\u1ec7c ti\u1ebfp theo l\u00e0 l\u1ef1a ch\u1ecdn c\u00f4ng c\u1ee5 hi\u1ec7u qu\u1ea3. \n\nS\u00e1ch l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t trong s\u1ed1 \u00edt l\u1ef1a ch\u1ecdn t\u1ea1o ra tr\u00ed tu\u1ec7 th\u1ef1c s\u1ef1. \nGi\u1ed1ng nh\u01b0 m\u00f3n \u0103n hay trang ph\u1ee5c, s\u00e1ch \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c chia th\u00e0nh nhi\u1ec1u th\u1ec3 lo\u1ea1i.\nC\u00f3 lo\u1ea1i ta th\u00edch v\u00e0 kh\u00f4ng th\u00edch. C\u00f3 lo\u1ea1i \u0111\u1ecdc c\u1ea3 ng\u00e0y kh\u00f4ng ch\u00e1n, v\u00e0 c\u00f3 lo\u1ea1i \u0111\u1ecdc hai trang \u0111\u00e3 bu\u1ed3n ng\u1ee7. \n\u0110\u1ecdc s\u00e1ch l\u00e0 t\u1ed1t, d\u00f9 \u0111\u00f3 l\u00e0 b\u1ea5t c\u1ee9 th\u1ec3 lo\u1ea1i n\u00e0o, nh\u01b0ng n\u1ebfu ch\u1ec9 \u0111\u1ecdc th\u1ec3 lo\u1ea1i ta th\u00edch th\u00ec ch\u00ednh ta \u0111\u00e3 gi\u1edbi h\u1ea1n kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng c\u1ee7a b\u1ea3n th\u00e2n. \n\nT\u1ea5t nhi\u00ean \u0111\u1ecdc ti\u1ec3u thuy\u1ebft s\u1ebd h\u1ea5p d\u1eabn h\u01a1n l\u00e0 s\u00e1ch khoa h\u1ecdc, tri\u1ebft h\u1ecdc, t\u00e2m l\u00fd h\u1ecdc... v\u1ed1n kh\u00f4 khan h\u01a1n, nh\u01b0ng nh\u1eefng ki\u1ebfn th\u1ee9c trong \u0111\u00f3 \u0111em t\u1edbi cho b\u1ea1n hai l\u1ee3i \u00edch:\n1.
